BattleScript_ParameterizedEffectHit:
copyarray vDynamicScriptData, Data_ParameterizedEffectHit, 0x8
goto BattleScript_Parameterized

BattleScript_ParameterizedEffectAltTypeCalcHit:
attackcanceler
attackstring
copyarray vDynamicScriptData, Data_ParameterizedEffectAltTypeCalcHit, 0x8
ppreduce
attackcanceler
accuracycheck BattleScript_MoveMissedPause, ACC_CURR_MOVE
goto BattleScript_Parameterized

BattleScript_ParameterizedStatUp:
copyarray vDynamicScriptData, Data_ParameterizedStatUpHit, 0x8
goto BattleScript_Parameterized

BattleScript_ParameterizedStatDown:
copyarray vDynamicScriptData, Data_ParameterizedStatDownHit, 0x8
goto BattleScript_Parameterized

BattleScript_ParameterizedStatDownPerfectAccuracy:
copyarray vDynamicScriptData, Data_ParameterizedStatDownHitPerfectAccuracy, 0x8
goto BattleScript_Parameterized

Data_ParameterizedEffectHit:
cEFFECT_CHOOSER
BattleScript_ParameterizedEffectHit_SetMoveEffect2

Data_ParameterizedEffectAltTypeCalcHit:
cEFFECT_CHOOSER
BattleScript_ParameterizedEffectAltTypeCalcHit_DoTypeCalc

Data_ParameterizedStatUp:
sSTATCHANGER
BattleScript_EffectStatUp

Data_ParameterizedStatDown:
sSTATCHANGER
BattleScript_EffectStatDown

Data_ParameterizedStatDownPerfectAccuracy:
sSTATCHANGER
BattleScript_ParameterizedStatDownPerfectAccuracy_CheckSubstitute

BattleScript_Parameterized:
jumpifbyte CMP_EQUAL, gBattlerAttacker, B_POSITION_PLAYER_LEFT, BattleScript_Parameterized_PlayerLeft
jumpifbyte CMP_EQUAL, gBattlerAttacker, B_POSITION_OPPONENT_LEFT, BattleScript_Parameterized_OpponentLeft
jumpifbyte CMP_EQUAL, gBattlerAttacker, B_POSITION_PLAYER_RIGHT, BattleScript_Parameterized_PlayerRight
// opponent right
copyhword vCurMove, gCurrentMove
goto BattleScript_Parameterized_SetMoveEffect

BattleScript_Parameterized_PlayerLeft:
copyhword vCurMove, gCurrentMove
goto BattleScript_Parameterized_SetMoveEffect

BattleScript_Parameterized_OpponentLeft:
copyhword vCurMove, gCurrentMove
goto BattleScript_Parameterized_SetMoveEffect

BattleScript_Parameterized_PlayerRight:
copyhword vCurMove, gCurrentMove
goto BattleScript_Parameterized_SetMoveEffect

BattleScript_Parameterized_SetMoveEffect:
copyarray vDynamicScript, BattleScript_Parameterized_EffectFromTable_Dynamic, 0x11
copybyte vDynamicScript[5], HIGH_BYTE(vCurMove) // manipulates a script, already factored into the way the code here is displayed
copybyte vDynamicScript[0xB], LOW_BYTE(vCurMove) // manipulates a script, already factored into the way the code here is displayed
call vDynamicScript
copyarray vDynamicScript, BattleScript_Parameterized_SetEffectByte_Dynamic, 0x11
copybyte vDynamicScript[5], vMoveEffect // manipulates a script, already factored into the way the code here is displayed
copyword vDynamicScript[7], vDynamicScriptData[0] // manipulates a script, already factored into the way the code here is displayed
copyword vDynamicScript[0xD], vDynamicScriptData[1] // manipulates a script, already factored into the way the code here is displayed
goto vDynamicScript

BattleScript_Parameterized_EffectFromTable_Dynamic:
addbyte vDynamicScript[0xC], HIGH_BYTE(vCurMove) // manipulates this script, already factored into the way the code here is displayed
copybyte vMoveEffect, Data_Parameterized_EffectTable[vCurMove]
return

BattleScript_Parameterized_SetEffectByte_Dynamic:
orbyte vDynamicScript[0xB], vMoveEffect // manipulates this script, already factored into the way the code here is displayed
setbyte vDynamicScriptData[0], vMoveEffect
goto vDynamicScriptData[1]

BattleScript_ParameterizedStatDownPerfectAccuracy_CheckSubstitute:
jumpifstatus2 BS_TARGET, STATUS2_SUBSTITUTE, BattleScript_ButItFailedAtkStringPpReduce
goto BattleScript_EffectStatDown_FromAttackString // skips accuracy check

BattleScript_DamageAndEffect (pj): @1052A00
04 05 06 07 09 0A 0E 5C 00 3A 0B 00 0C 00 0D 12 40 00 0F 12 40 00 19 00 00 00 00 00 00 20 00 01 10 00 2F 2A 05 09 20 00 00 11 00 0A A9 1B 08 29 04 2C 3D 02 02 29 0A A9 1B 08 3C

typecalc

waitanimation

waitstate

datahpupdate BS_TARGET

waitmessage 0x40

// if_hp_zero BS_TARGET, BattleScript_MoveEnd
jumpifstat BS_TARGET, CMP_NOT_EQUAL, 0x10, 0, BattleScript_ClearSmog_CheckImmunity
jumpifstat BS_TARGET, CMP_EQUAL, 0x11, 0, BattleScript_MoveEnd

BattleScript_ClearSmog_CheckImmunity:
jumpifmovehadnoeffect BattleScript_MoveEnd
return

BattleScript_ClearSmog:
jumpifstatus2 BS_TARGET, STATUS2_SUBSTITUTE, BattleScript_MoveEnd
setbyte sMOVEEND_STATE, 0x0
moveend 0x0, 0x0
// if_hp_zero BS_ATTACKER, BattleScript_MakeMoveMissed
jumpifstat BS_ATTACKER, CMP_NOT_EQUAL, 0x10, 0, BattleScript_ClearSmog_DoEffect
jumpifstat BS_ATTACKER, CMP_EQUAL, 0x11, 0, BattleScript_MakeMoveMissed

BattleScript_ClearSmog_DoEffect:
jumpifbyte CMP_EQUAL, gBattlerTarget, B_POSITION_PLAYER_LEFT, BattleScript_ClearSmog_PlayerLeft
jumpifbyte CMP_EQUAL, gBattlerTarget, B_POSITION_OPPONENT_LEFT, BattleScript_ClearSmog_OpponentLeft
jumpifbyte CMP_EQUAL, gBattlerTarget, B_POSITION_PLAYER_RIGHT, BattleScript_ClearSmog_PlayerRight

goto BattleScript_ClearSmog_Message

BattleScript_ClearSmog_PlayerLeft:
copyarray gBattleMons[B_POSITION_PLAYER_LEFT].statStages, Data_Haze_AllStatLevelsZero, 0x8
goto BattleScript_ClearSmog_Message

BattleScript_ClearSmog_OpponentLeft:
copyarray gBattleMons[B_POSITION_OPPONENT_LEFT].statStages, Data_Haze_AllStatLevelsZero, 0x8
goto BattleScript_ClearSmog_Message

BattleScript_ClearSmog_PlayerRight:
copyarray gBattleMons[B_POSITION_PLAYER_RIGHT].statStages, Data_Haze_AllStatLevelsZero, 0x8
goto BattleScript_ClearSmog_Message

BattleScript_ClearSmog_Message:
printstring STRINGID_PKMNSSTATCHANGESREMOVED
waitmessage 0x40
end

BattleScript_Phaze_CanSwitch:
setbyte sMOVEEND_STATE, 0x0
moveend 0x0, 0x0
// if_hp_zero BS_ATTACKER, BattleScript_MakeMoveMissed
jumpifstat BS_ATTACKER, CMP_NOT_EQUAL, 0x10, 0, BattleScript_Phaze_DragonTail

BattleScript_Phaze_DragonTail:

jumpifstatus3condition BS_TARGET, STATUS3_ROOTED, BattleScript_PrintMonIsRooted

BattleScript_Phaze_CheckIfCanSwitch:

goto BattleScript_Phaze_CanSwitch

BattleScript_Phaze_GetAttackerLevel:
copyarray vDynamicScript, BattleScript_Phaze_CheckLevels, 0xC
jumpifbyte CMP_EQUAL, gBattlerAttacker, B_POSITION_PLAYER_LEFT, BattleScript_Phaze_GetPlayerLeftLevel
jumpifbyte CMP_EQUAL, gBattlerAttacker, B_POSITION_OPPONENT_LEFT, BattleScript_Phaze_GetOpponentLeftLevel
jumpifbyte CMP_EQUAL, gBattlerAttacker, B_POSITION_PLAYER_RIGHT, BattleScript_Phaze_GetPlayerRightLevel
copybyte vDynamicScript[6], gBattleMons[B_POSITION_OPPONENT_RIGHT].level
goto BattleScript_Phaze_GetTargetLevel

BattleScript_Phaze_GetPlayerLeftLevel:
copybyte vDynamicScript[6], gBattleMons[B_POSITION_PLAYER_LEFT].level
goto BattleScript_Phaze_GetTargetLevel

BattleScript_Phaze_GetOpponentLeftLevel:
copybyte vDynamicScript[6], gBattleMons[B_POSITION_OPPONENT_LEFT].level
goto BattleScript_Phaze_GetTargetLevel

BattleScript_Phaze_GetPlayerRightLevel:
copybyte vDynamicScript[6], gBattleMons[B_POSITION_PLAYER_RIGHT].level
goto BattleScript_Phaze_GetTargetLevel

BattleScript_Phaze_GetTargetLevel:
jumpifbyte CMP_EQUAL, gBattlerTarget, B_POSITION_PLAYER_LEFT, BattleScript_Phaze_GetPlayerLeftLevelAddress
jumpifbyte CMP_EQUAL, gBattlerTarget, B_POSITION_OPPONENT_LEFT, BattleScript_Phaze_GetOpponentLeftLevelAddress
jumpifbyte CMP_EQUAL, gBattlerTarget, B_POSITION_PLAYER_RIGHT, BattleScript_Phaze_GetPlayerRightLevelAddress
copyword vDynamicScript[2], [OPPONENT_RIGHT_LEVEL_ADDRESS] // gBattleMons[B_POSITION_OPPONENT_RIGHT].level
goto vDynamicScript

BattleScript_Phaze_GetPlayerLeftLevelAddress:
copyword vDynamicScript[2], [PLAYER_LEFT_LEVEL_ADDRESS] // gBattleMons[B_POSITION_PLAYER_LEFT].level
goto vDynamicScript

BattleScript_Phaze_GetOpponentLeftLevelAddress:
copyword vDynamicScript[2], [OPPONENT_LEFT_LEVEL_ADDRESS] // gBattleMons[B_POSITION_OPPONENT_LEFT].level
goto vDynamicScript

BattleScript_Phaze_GetPlayerRightLevelAddress:
copyword vDynamicScript[2], [PLAYER_RIGHT_LEVEL_ADDRESS] // gBattleMons[B_POSITION_PLAYER_RIGHT].level
goto vDynamicScript

BattleScript_Phaze_CheckLevels:
jumpifbyte CMP_GREATER_THAN, vDynamicScript[2], vDynamicScript[6], BattleScript_MoveEnd
return

BattleScript_SpAtkOrSpeedUpHit_TargetHasntMoved:
setmoveeffect MOVE_EFFECT_SP_ATK_PLUS_1 | MOVE_EFFECT_AFFECTS_USER | MOVE_EFFECT_CERTAIN
goto BattleScript_HitFromAtkCanceler

BattleScript_SpAtkOrSpeedUpHit_TargetAlreadyMoved:
setmoveeffect MOVE_EFFECT_SPEED_PLUS_1 | MOVE_EFFECT_AFFECTS_USER | MOVE_EFFECT_CERTAIN
goto BattleScript_HitFromAtkCanceler

BattleScript_SpAtkOrSpeedUpHit_CheckTargetTurn:
jumpifbyteequal gBattlerByTurnOrder[0], gBattlerTarget, BattleScript_SpAtkOrSpeedUpHit_TargetGoesFirst
jumpifbyteequal gBattlerByTurnOrder[1], gBattlerTarget, BattleScript_SpAtkOrSpeedUpHit_TargetGoesSecond
jumpifbyteequal gBattlerByTurnOrder[2], gBattlerTarget, BattleScript_SpAtkOrSpeedUpHit_TargetGoesThird
jumpifbyteequal gBattlerByTurnOrder[3], gBattlerTarget, BattleScript_SpAtkOrSpeedUpHit_TargetGoesFourth

BattleScript_SpAtkOrSpeedUpHit_TargetGoesFirst:
setbyte vDynamicScript[6], 0
goto vDynamicScript

BattleScript_SpAtkOrSpeedUpHit_TargetGoesSecond:
setbyte vDynamicScript[6], 1
goto vDynamicScript

BattleScript_SpAtkOrSpeedUpHit_TargetGoesThird:
setbyte vDynamicScript[6], 2
goto vDynamicScript

BattleScript_SpAtkOrSpeedUpHit_TargetGoesFourth:
setbyte vDynamicScript[6], 3
goto vDynamicScript

goto BattleScript_PaybackAndHitsSteelDouble_CheckIfOpponentRightMovesLast

BattleScript_EffectDoubleDamageOnStatus_ActualScript:

attackstring

jumpifmove MOVE_SMELLING_SALTS, BattleScript_DoubleDamageAndCureParalysis
jumpifmove MOVE_WAKE_UP_SLAP, BattleScript_DoubleDamageAndCureSleep
jumpifmove 0x283, BattleScript_DoubleDamageAndCurePoison
jumpifmove 0x266, BattleScript_DoubleDamageAndCureBurn

goto BattleScript_DoubleDamageAndCureAttract

BattleScript_DoubleDamageOnAnyStatus:

BattleScript_DoubleDamageAndCureParalysis:

BattleScript_DoubleDamageAndCureSleep:

BattleScript_DoubleDamageAndCurePoison:

goto BattleScript_DoubleDamageAndCureStatus_RemoveStatus

BattleScript_DoubleDamageAndCureBurn:

goto BattleScript_EffectHit

BattleScript_DoubleDamageAndCureBurn_Burned:

goto BattleScript_DoubleDamageAndCureStatus_RemoveStatus

BattleScript_DoubleDamageAndCureFreeze:

goto BattleScript_EffectHit

BattleScript_DoubleDamageAndCureFreeze_Frozen:

goto BattleScript_DoubleDamageAndCureStatus_RemoveStatus

BattleScript_DoubleDamageAndCureStatus_RemoveStatus:

goto BattleScript_SmellingSaltsDoubleDmg // old script 2x damage point

// ??? always doubled damage?
BattleScript_DoubleDamageAndCureAttract:
ppreduce
setbyte sDMG_MULTIPLIER, 2
critcalc
damagecalc
typecalc
adjustnormaldamage
jumpifbyte CMP_COMMON_BITS, gMoveResultFlags, MOVE_RESULT_NO_EFFECT, BattleScript_HitFromAtkAnimation
attackanimation
waitanimation
effectivenesssound
hitanimation BS_TARGET
waitstate
healthbarupdate BS_TARGET
datahpupdate BS_TARGET
critmessage
waitmessage 0x40
resultmessage
waitmessage 0x40
tryfaintmon BS_TARGET, FALSE, NULL
// if_hp_zero BS_TARGET, BattleScript_MoveEnd
jumpifstat BS_TARGET, CMP_NOT_EQUAL, 0x10, 0, BattleScript_DoubleDamageAndCureAttract_CureAttract
jumpifstat BS_TARGET, CMP_EQUAL, 0x11, 0, BattleScript_MoveEnd

BattleScript_DoubleDamageAndCureAttract_CureAttract:
jumpifbyte CMP_EQUAL, gBattlerTarget, B_POSITION_PLAYER_LEFT, BattleScript_DoubleDamageAndCureAttract_PlayerLeft
jumpifbyte CMP_EQUAL, gBattlerTarget, B_POSITION_OPPONENT_LEFT, BattleScript_DoubleDamageAndCureAttract_OpponentLeft
jumpifbyte CMP_EQUAL, gBattlerTarget, B_POSITION_PLAYER_RIGHT, BattleScript_DoubleDamageAndCureAttract_PlayerRight
jumpifbyte CMP_EQUAL, gBattlerTarget, B_POSITION_OPPONENT_RIGHT, BattleScript_DoubleDamageAndCureAttract_OpponentRight

BattleScript_DoubleDamageAndCureAttract_PlayerLeft:
bicword gBattleMons[B_POSITION_PLAYER_LEFT].status2, STATUS2_INFATUATION
goto BattleScript_DoubleDamageAndCureAttract_PrintString

BattleScript_DoubleDamageAndCureAttract_OpponentLeft:
bicword gBattleMons[B_POSITION_OPPONENT_LEFT].status2, STATUS2_INFATUATION
goto BattleScript_DoubleDamageAndCureAttract_PrintString

BattleScript_DoubleDamageAndCureAttract_PlayerRight:
bicword gBattleMons[B_POSITION_PLAYER_RIGHT].status2, STATUS2_INFATUATION
goto BattleScript_DoubleDamageAndCureAttract_PrintString

BattleScript_DoubleDamageAndCureAttract_OpponentRight:
bicword gBattleMons[B_POSITION_OPPONENT_RIGHT].status2, STATUS2_INFATUATION
goto BattleScript_DoubleDamageAndCureAttract_PrintString

BattleScript_DoubleDamageAndCureAttract_PrintString:
copyarray gBattleTextBuff1, gText_Love, 0x5
printstring STRINGID_PKMNHEALEDOFSTATUS
waitmessage 0x40
goto BattleScript_MoveEnd

BattleScript_DoubleDamageIfPoisoned:
jumpifstatus BS_TARGET, STATUS1_POISON, BattleScript_EffectHit_DoubleDamage // not toxic?
goto BattleScript_EffectHit

BattleScript_DoVenomDrenchEffect:
jumpifstat BS_TARGET, CMP_GREATER_THAN, STAT_ATK, 0, BattleScript_VenomDrench_Animation

BattleScript_VenomDrench_TryLowerSpeed:

BattleScript_LowerOneOfMultipleStats:

jumpifbyte CMP_EQUAL, gHasPlayedStatAnimation, TRUE, BattleScript_LowerOneOfMultipleStats_PrintMessage
setgraphicalstatchangevalues
playanimation BS_TARGET, B_ANIM_STATS_CHANGE, sB_ANIM_ARG1
orbyte gHasPlayedStatAnimation, TRUE

BattleScript_LowerOneOfMultipleStats_PrintMessage:
printfromtable gStatDownStringIds
waitmessage 0x40

BattleScript_LowerOneOfMultipleStats_End:
return

BattleScript_TripleKickLoop:
jumpifhasnohp BS_ATTACKER, BattleScript_TripleKickEnd
jumpifhasnohp BS_TARGET, BattleScript_TripleKickNoMoreHits
jumpifhalfword CMP_EQUAL, gChosenMove, MOVE_SLEEP_TALK, BattleScript_DoTripleKickAttack

addbyte sTRIPLE_KICK_POWER, 10
addbyte sMULTIHIT_STRING + 4, 0x1

damagecalc
typecalc
adjustnormaldamage

waitanimation
effectivenesssound

waitstate

BattleScript_TripleKickNoMoreHits:

jumpifbyte CMP_EQUAL, sMULTIHIT_STRING + 4, 0x0, BattleScript_TripleKickPrintStrings

BattleScript_TripleKickPrintStrings:

waitmessage 0x40
jumpifbyte CMP_EQUAL, sMULTIHIT_STRING + 4, 0x0, BattleScript_TripleKickEnd
jumpifbyte CMP_COMMON_BITS, gMoveResultFlags, MOVE_RESULT_DOESNT_AFFECT_FOE, BattleScript_TripleKickEnd
copyarray gBattleTextBuff1, sMULTIHIT_STRING, 0x6
printstring STRINGID_HITXTIMES
waitmessage 0x40

BattleScript_TripleKickEnd:
seteffectwithchance
tryfaintmon BS_TARGET, FALSE, NULL
setbyte sMOVEEND_STATE, 0xE
moveend 0x0, 0x0
end

BattleScript_DoDamageFunction (pj): @1053C00

jumpifbyte CMP_EQUAL, gBattlerAttacker, B_POSITION_OPPONENT_LEFT, BattleScript_Thief_IsOpponent

BattleScript_Thief_IsOpponent:
jumpifbyte CMP_EQUAL, gBattleTypeFlags, MOVE_RESULT_NOT_VERY_EFFECTIVE, BattleScript_HitFromAtkCanceler
call BattleScript_DoDamageFunction
jumpifstatus2 BS_TARGET, STATUS2_SUBSTITUTE, BattleScript_HitFromTryFaintMon
jumpifability BS_TARGET, ABILITY_STICKY_HOLD, BattleScript_Thief_StickyHoldMsg
jumpifitem BS_TARGET, ITEM_NONE, ATKFC_NOT_EQUAL, BattleScript_HitFromTryFaintMon
jumpifitem BS_ATTACKER, ITEM_NONE, ATKFC_EQUAL, BattleScript_HitFromTryFaintMon
jumpifbyte CMP_EQUAL, gBattlerTarget, B_POSITION_PLAYER_LEFT, BattleScript_Thief_PlayerLeft
jumpifbyte CMP_EQUAL, gBattlerTarget, B_POSITION_OPPONENT_LEFT, BattleScript_Thief_OpponentLeft
jumpifbyte CMP_EQUAL, gBattlerTarget, B_POSITION_PLAYER_RIGHT, BattleScript_Thief_PlayerRight

goto BattleScript_Thief_PlayAnimation

BattleScript_Thief_OpponentLeft:

goto BattleScript_Thief_PlayAnimation

BattleScript_Thief_PlayerRight:
copyhword gLastUsedItem, gBattleMons[B_POSITION_PLAYER_RIGHT].item
goto BattleScript_Thief_PlayAnimation

BattleScript_Thief_PlayAnimation:

copyhword gStringVar4, (gBattlerAttacker, gBattlerTarget)
copybyte gBattlerAttacker, gBattlerTarget
copybyte gBattlerTarget, gStringVar4
tryswapitems BattleScript_Thief_PrintString

BattleScript_Thief_PrintString:
copyhword (gBattlerAttacker, gBattlerTarget), gStringVar4
printstring STRINGID_PKMNSTOLEITEM
waitmessage 0x40
goto BattleScript_HitFromTryFaintMon

BattleScript_Thief_StickyHoldMsg:
printstring 0x214
waitmessage 0x40
goto BattleScript_HitFromTryFaintMon

accuracycheck BattleScript_MoveMissedPause, ACC_CURR_MOVE
critcalc
damagecalc
typecalc
adjustnormaldamage
attackanimation
waitanimation
effectivenesssound
hitanimation BS_TARGET
waitstate
healthbarupdate BS_TARGET
datahpupdate BS_TARGET
critmessage
waitmessage 0x40
resultmessage
waitmessage 0x40
jumpifbyte CMP_COMMON_BITS, gMoveResultFlags, MOVE_RESULT_NO_EFFECT, BattleScript_HitFromTryFaintMon

goto BattleScript_UTurn_CheckFailed

BattleScript_UTurn_MonFainted:
jumpifcantswitch ATK4F_DONT_CHECK_STATUSES | BS_TARGET, BattleScript_MoveEnd
goto BattleScript_UTurn_TrySwitch

BattleScript_UTurn_CheckFailed:

BattleScript_UTurn_TrySwitch:

goto BattleScript_UTurn_PursuitSwitchDmgLoop

BattleScript_UTurn_PursuitSwitchDmgSetMultihit:
setmultihit 0x2

BattleScript_UTurn_PursuitSwitchDmgLoop:
jumpifnopursuitswitchdmg BattleScript_UTurn_NoPursuit
swapattackerwithtarget
trysetdestinybondtohappen
call BattleScript_PursuitDmgOnSwitchOut
swapattackerwithtarget

BattleScript_UTurn_NoPursuit:
setbyte sDMG_MULTIPLIER, 0x1
goto BattleScript_UTurn_DoSwitchOut

BattleScript_UTurn_Unused:

openpartyscreen 0x1, BattleScript_MoveEnd

switchinanim BS_ATTACKER, FALSE
waitstate
switchineffects BS_ATTACKER

bichalfword gChosenMove, 0xFFFF
goto BattleScript_MoveEnd

BattleScript_EffectWorkUp (pj): @80B330
00 02 03 20 01 03 01 0C 45 B3 80 08 20 01 00 04 0C A3 C5 1B 08 09 0A 2E 3F 3F 02 02 00 48 01 12 00 2E 3E 3F 02 02 11 89 41 70 B3 80 08 29 00 E7 3D 02 02 02 70 B3 80 08 13 48 45 3C 08 12 40 00 2E 3E 3F 02 02 14 89 41 8F B3 80 08 29 00 E7 3D 02 02 02 8F B3 80 08 13 48 45 3C 08 12 40 00 28 0A A9 1B 08

BattleScript_EffectAtkAndSpAtkUp_ActualScript:
jumpifmove MOVE_GROWTH, BattleScript_EffectGrowth
jumpifmove MOVE_ENERGIZE, BattleScript_EffectEnergize
goto BattleScript_EffectWorkUp

BattleScript_EffectGrowth:
jumpifhalfword CMP_COMMON_BITS, gBattleWeather, WEATHER_SUN_TEMPORARY, BattleScript_GrowthInSun
jumpifhalfword CMP_COMMON_BITS, gBattleWeather, WEATHER_SUN_ANY, BattleScript_GrowthInSun
goto BattleScript_EffectWorkUp

BattleScript_GrowthInSun:
attackcanceler
attackstring
ppreduce
jumpifstat BS_ATTACKER, CMP_LESS_THAN, STAT_ATK, 0xC, BattleScript_GrowthInSun_DoMoveAnim
jumpifstat BS_ATTACKER, CMP_EQUAL, STAT_SPATK, 0xC, BattleScript_CantRaiseMultipleStats

BattleScript_GrowthInSun_DoMoveAnim:
attackanimation
waitanimation
setbyte sSTAT_ANIM_PLAYED, FALSE
playstatchangeanimation BS_ATTACKER, BIT_ATK | BIT_DEF, 0x0 // wrong, should be 0x12, 0x2 = BIT_ATK | BIT_SPATK, ATK48_STAT_BY_TWO
setstatchanger STAT_ATK, 2, FALSE
statbuffchange MOVE_EFFECT_AFFECTS_USER | 0x1, BattleScript_GrowthInSun_TrySpAtk
jumpifbyte CMP_EQUAL, cMULTISTRING_CHOOSER, 0x2, BattleScript_GrowthInSun_TrySpAtk
printfromtable gStatUpStringIds
waitmessage 0x40

BattleScript_GrowthInSun_TrySpAtk:
setstatchanger STAT_SPATK, 2, FALSE
statbuffchange MOVE_EFFECT_AFFECTS_USER | 0x1, BattleScript_GrowthInSun_End
jumpifbyte CMP_EQUAL, cMULTISTRING_CHOOSER, 0x2, BattleScript_GrowthInSun_End
printfromtable gStatUpStringIds
waitmessage 0x40

BattleScript_GrowthInSun_End:
goto BattleScript_MoveEnd

BattleScript_EffectEnergize:
jumpifhalfword CMP_COMMON_BITS, gBattleWeather, WEATHER_RAIN_TEMPORARY, BattleScript_GrowthInSun
jumpifhalfword CMP_COMMON_BITS, gBattleWeather, WEATHER_RAIN_ANY, BattleScript_GrowthInSun
goto BattleScript_EffectWorkUp

BattleScript_EffectWorkUp:
attackcanceler
attackstring
ppreduce
jumpifstat BS_ATTACKER, CMP_LESS_THAN, STAT_ATK, 0xC, BattleScript_WorkUp_DoMoveAnim
jumpifstat BS_ATTACKER, CMP_EQUAL, STAT_SPATK, 0xC, BattleScript_CantRaiseMultipleStats

BattleScript_WorkUp_DoMoveAnim:
attackanimation
waitanimation
setbyte sSTAT_ANIM_PLAYED, FALSE
playstatchangeanimation BS_ATTACKER, BIT_ATK | BIT_SPATK, 0x0
setstatchanger STAT_ATK, 1, FALSE
statbuffchange MOVE_EFFECT_AFFECTS_USER | 0x1, BattleScript_WorkUp_TrySpAtk
jumpifbyte CMP_EQUAL, cMULTISTRING_CHOOSER, 0x2, BattleScript_WorkUp_TrySpAtk
printfromtable gStatUpStringIds
waitmessage 0x40

BattleScript_WorkUp_TrySpAtk:
setstatchanger STAT_SPATK, 1, FALSE
statbuffchange MOVE_EFFECT_AFFECTS_USER | 0x1, BattleScript_WorkUp_End
jumpifbyte CMP_EQUAL, cMULTISTRING_CHOOSER, 0x2, BattleScript_WorkUp_End
printfromtable gStatUpStringIds
waitmessage 0x40

BattleScript_WorkUp_End:
goto BattleScript_MoveEnd
